As of my last update in April 2023, Facebook doesn't offer a feature that allows you to display one post exclusively to your friends and a different post to everyone else who isn't your friend. However, Facebook does provide various privacy settings for posts, such as:Public: Visible to anyone, including people not on your friends list.Friends: Only visible to people you are friends with on Facebook.Custom: Allows you to include or exclude specific people from viewing the post.These settings can be adjusted for each post you make, but they don't allow for simultaneously showing different content to different groups (friends vs. non-friends) with a single post. If you want to share different content with different groups, you would need to make separate posts with different privacy settings.YouSo I guess it is difficult or not possible. This would be visible to everyone, including non-friends.Create a Custom Post: Then, for the content you want to share only with non-friends, you could create another post and use the "Custom" privacy setting. Here, you can manually exclude each of your friends.
